  * grade_story_10.txt (grade=9.1)
    The abandoned spaceport customs office creates an evocative liminal space that perfectly mirrors the character's transitional state. The sensory details are exceptional—the "hum of server rooms" through "corroded walls," the "acid-yellow clouds," and the tactile experience of swallowing the koji that "seared her throat." The science fiction elements blend seamlessly with the emotional journey, creating a world where biological mutations serve as perfect metaphors for psychological transformation. The atmosphere of decay and renewal permeates every description.
